As a result, the air conditioner did not cool on the first day of check-in. They said they didn't know when it would be repaired, so they moved us to the annex building and upgraded us to room 8910 with two rooms for free. The room is 110 square meters, with two bedrooms, two bathrooms and two living rooms, as well as a washer-dryer (no laundry detergent provided) and a microwave. It was very comfortable. Sakura chocolate was also given as a gift on the first day of check-in. To have breakfast, you need to take the elevator to the negative second floor, then walk to the main building and take the elevator to the negative first floor. Because it is inside the building and the road is flat, it is not a big problem. Originally, we only stayed for four nights. Due to the rain, the booked travel plan was not completed. We extended for two more nights. As a result, the hotel turned off the air conditioner because of the rain and the weather turned cooler. The windows in the room could not be opened wide, and there were mosquitoes. Although it was quite cool outside, the hotel room was very stuffy. As a five-star hotel, I think the hotel should provide various facilities and services as usual, so that guests have the right to choose independently, instead of directly shutting them down.
The hotel is not far from Nanchang Street and Nanchan Temple. There are many buses at the door. The road conditions are also good, there is no traffic jam, and it is convenient to go to the attractions. The subway station is on Nanchan Temple Pedestrian Street, a little distance away.
Breakfast starts at 6:30 and ends at 10:00. It is very friendly for guests who are going out early. The breakfast room is clean and a**ospheric, and the breakfast is rich.
The hotel staff are very warm and friendly!

msg:Temporarily decided to come to Wuxi for fun, and chose Rocas Hotel after screening according to my son's requirements. I have to say that this time the choice is correct.

For travelers, the convenient transportation around the hotel is the first choice. Take Exit 8 of Nanchan Temple on Line 1, walk through a variety of night markets, and walk for 10 minutes to the hotel.

The hotel has a stylish appearance and is divided into two buildings: a boutique hotel and a service hotel. This time we booked a service-style senior suite. The front desk immediately upgraded the room type when we saw us with our children. He also enthusiastically told us the route to the room, breakfast and the location of the swimming pool.
The decoration of the room is simple and bright, with brand-new facilities and all kinds of kitchen supplies; the design of one bedroom and one living room is very suitable for a family of three.

The breakfast and swimming pool gym are located on the B1 floor of the boutique hotel. The rectangular swimming pool is very large and the water is very clean, which is suitable for children to play in summer vacation. Although there are not many varieties of breakfast, there are both Chinese and Western styles. The head chef will personally deliver the meals and ask if the dishes are suitable for our appetite, which made us feel very kind. The vegetable salad and fruit are packed in glass jars, which are very delicate and make people feel appetizing instantly.

Opposite the hotel is the famous Nanchang Street, the scenery at night is even more charming; the night market at the nearby Nanchan Temple is the favorite of young people. The No. 15 road at the entrance can also go directly to Huishan Ancient Town, which is very convenient.

We stayed for 2 nights, whether it was the warm and smiling service of all the staff we met in the hotel, or the convenience of traveling in the hotel, we were deeply impressed.
